🚀 nORM Performance Benchmarks
==============================

This benchmark compares nORM against:
• Entity Framework Core
• Dapper
• Raw ADO.NET

Test scenarios:
• Single inserts
• Simple queries (standard & compiled/prepared)
• Complex queries with filtering (standard & compiled/prepared)
• Joins
• Count operations
• Bulk operations (naive, batched, idiomatic)

⚠️  This will take several minutes to complete.
